PHYIR; RTZA BAR, CHOS SKU MDZAD PA DANG BCAS PA, ,ZHES PA'I\
DGONGS PA YIN PA'I PHYIR, 'GREL CHEN LAS, YE SHES KHO NA DANG\
MDZAD PAR SBYAR BA'I PHYIR DE SKAD DU GSUNGS TE ZHES GSUNGS PA'I\
PHYIR, YANG KHA CIG NA RE, DE BZHIN\
\
NAM PA'I DE SGRA SPRUL SKU LA SBYOR MI RIGS PAR THAL, SLOB DPON\
GYIS YE SHES CHOS SKU DANG SBYAR BA'I PHYIR NA RNAM PA GCIG TU\
MA KHYAB STE, SLOB DPON GYIS MDOR BSTAN DANG, CHOS KYI SKU YI\
'PHRIN LAS NI, ,ZHES PA'I CHOS SKU YE\
\
SHES GTZO BO'I DBANG DU BYAS PA'I PHYIR, GSER 'PHRENG LAS, DE\
BZHIN NI SLOB DPON LTAR NA CHOS SKU YIN LA 'PHAGS PA LTAR NA\
SPRUL SKU YIN PAR BSHAD LA ZHES GSUNGS PA'I PHYIR, RTZA BAR 'DOD\
MI NUS TE, RTZA BA'I 'BREL BYAS\
\
NA SPRUL SKU DANG SBYOR DGOS PA'I PHYIR, RTZA BAR, THUB PA'I\
SPRUL SKU RGYUN MI 'CHAD, ,DE BZHIN ZHES GSUNGS PA'I PHYIR TE,\
RNAM BSHAD LAS, RTZA BA'I 'GREL GYI DBANG DU BYAS NA DE BZHIN\
ZHES PA SPRUL SKU DANG 'BREL YANG SLOB DPON\
\
@066B KYIS CHOS SKU LA MDZAD DO ZHES GSUNGS PA'I PHYIR, YANG KHA\
CIG NA RE, SANGS RGYAS KYI 'PHRIN LAS YIN NA, LAM ZHUGS YAN CHAD\
NA YOD PAS KHYAB ZER NA, LAM MA ZHUGS KYI NGAN 'GRO GSUM LHA\
MI'I SDUG BSNGAL ZHI BAR\
\
MDZAD PA'I 'PHRIN LAS DE CHOS CAN, DER THAL, DE'I PHYIR, RTAGS\
GRUB STE, DE YOD PA'I PHYIR, 'GRO RNAMS ZHI BA'I LAS DANG NI,\
,ZHES GSUNGS PA'I PHYIR, KHYAB STE, GSER 'PHRENG LAS, NGAN SONG\
GSUM DANG LHA MI'I 'GRO BA\
\
RNAMS KYI SDUG BSNGAL ZHI BA BSGRUB PA'I LAS MDZAD PA ZHES\
GSUNGS PA'I PHYIR, DES SANGS RGYAS KYI 'PHRIN LAS LA 'GRO BA\
DRUG GI RGYUD DU YOD PAR SHES SO, ,YANG KHA CIG NA RE, SANGS\
RGYAS KYI 'PHRIN LAS YIN NA,\
\
LAM MA ZHUGS NA YOD PAS KHYAB ZER NA, 'PHRIN LAS LHAG MA NYER\
DRUG CHOS CAN, DER THAL, DE'I PHYIR, KHYAB PA KHAS, RTAGS SLA,\
'DOD MI NUS TE, LHAG MA NYER DRUG LAM LA BKOD PA'I 'PHRIN LAS\
YIN PA'I PHYIR,\
\
DER THAL, TSOGS LAM LA 'GOD PA'I GSUM, SBYOR LAM LA 'GOD PA'I\
BZHI DANG, MTHONG LAM LA 'GOD PA'I GCIG DANG, SGOM LAM LA 'GOD\
BA'I 'PHRIN LAS BCO BRGYAD YOD PA'I PHYIR, DANG PO GRUB STE,\
'GRO\
\
RNAMS ZHI BA'I LAS DANG NI, ,BSDU RNAM BZHI LA 'GOD PA DANG,\
,KUN NAS NYON MONGS BCAS PA YIS, ,RNAM PAR BYANG BA RTOGS PA\
DANG, ,ZHES SO, ,GNYIS PA GRUB STE, SEMS CAN RNAMS DON JI BZHIN\
GYI, ,DON DANG\
\
@067A *, ,PHA ROL PHYIN DRUG DANG, ,SANGS RGYAS LAM DANG RANG\
BZHIN GYIS, ,STONG BA NYID DANG ZHES SO, ,GSUM PA GRUB STE,\
GNYIS ZAD DANG, ,ZHES SO, ,BZHI PA GRUB STE, BRDA DANG DMIGS PA\
MED PA DANG, ,NAS,\
\
THA DAD YONGS SU MI SHES DANG, ,ZHES SO, ,LAM GYI MI GNAS PA'I\
MYANG 'DAS LA 'GOD PA'I DE YOD DE, MYA NGAN 'DAS LA DGOD PA STE,\
,ZHES SO, ,NYER BDUN YOD TSUL STON PAR, CHOS KYI SKU YI 'PHRIN\
LAS NI, ,RNAM PA NYI\
\
SHU BDUN DU BZHED, ,CES SO, ,'PHRIN LAS NYER BDUN YANG SRID\
MTHA'I BAR DU DAR ZHING RGYAS PAR 'GYUR BA YIN TE, 'GREL BA LAS,\
'DI'I 'PHRIN LAS RNAM PA NYI SHU RTZA BDUN YANG 'KHOR BA JI SRID\
PAR BZHED PA ZHES GSUNGS\
\
PA'I PHYIR, SMRAS PA, AE MA PHYOGS BCU'I RGYAL BA SRAS BCAS\
DANG, ,NYAN RANG THEG PA GSUM GYI TSOGS RNAMS KUN, ,SKYED MDZAD\
DUS GSUM THAR PAR BGROD PA'I LAM, ,GZHUNG LAM 'BRAS BU'I SHER\
PHYIN YUM\
\
RNAMS RMAD, ,KYE MA MDO SNGAGS GZHUNG MANG GRUB MTHA' KUN, ,YUN\
RING NGAL BRGYAS DUB PA'I NGAL BSO'I GNAS, ,PHAR PHYIN GZHUNG\
DON LEGS STON LAM RIM LAS, ,MDO SNGAGS LAM GYI SGO RNYED NGAL\
GSO THOB, ,\
\
RIGS BRGYA'I KHYAB BDAG SRE DA RDO RJE 'CHANG, ,MGON DE'I ZHABS\
BRTEN MDO SNGAGS GSANG BA'I GNAD, ,MA LUS KUN BSDUS KHRID CHEN\
AA MRi TA, ,KLU DBANG GRAGS THOB LEGS SMON DGA' BDES KHYAB,\
,LONGS SKRUL? MES\

@067B POS MNGAG PA'I LEGS BSHAD KYI, ,DAG BYED MCHOD YON SNGON\
BYON SHING RTA CHE'I, ,BLO GROS RAL BAR NYIS STONG LNGA BRGYAR?\
BZUNG, ,BDAG BLO SKAL LDAN SHING RTAS RGYUN 'DI BSGRENGS, ,'DIR\
'BAD DGE BA CHES DKAR MKHA' KHYAB\
\
'GRO'I, ,LEGS BYAS 'DAB BRGYA BYE BA'I TSOGS BZHAD CING, ,SKAL\
BZANG BUNG BAS DAR DIR MGRIN GLU DANG, ,LEGS BSHAD SNANG BAS CIG\
CAR KUN KHYAB SHOG ,RGYAL BA SRAS BCAS RNAMS KYI BYIN RLABS\
DANG, ,RTEN CING 'BREL\
\
'BYUNG BSLU MED BDEN PA'I MTHUS, ,CHOS 'DI PHYOGS DUS KUN TU\
RGYAS GYUR CIG ,CES PHAR PHYIN GYI MTHA' DPYOD BSAM 'PHEL YID\
BZHIN NOR BU'I 'PHRENG MDZES SKAL BZANG MIG 'BYED CES BYA BA 'DI\
NI GANGS CAN GYI PHYAG NA PAD\
\
DKAR 'CHANG BAS BKA' STZAL GYI ME TOG YANG GNANG ZHING, NYE CHAR\
MKHAS 'DUS DPAL LDAN BKRA SHIS SGO MANG GIS LAN GSUM CHOS GRVA\
KHANG CHEN KUN DANG GRVA RGAN 'DUL BA CHOS RJES DUNG DKAR GSER\
GSHOGS CAN DANG MKHA'\

'GRO MA THAMS CAD KYI GTZO MO LAB KYI SGRON MA'I DBU THOD RING\
BSREL CAN 'BRAS BU SNA TSOGS DANG SU WARnAS BRGYAN BA DANG BCAS,\
RAB 'BYAMS SMRA BA NGAG DBANG DGE 'DUN GYIS DKAR YOL MAndAL DANG\
BCAS, TSOGS KYI MAndAL\
\
RANG GI 'BUL TSAN DANG, KHYAD PAR MANG THOS MDO SNGAGS SMRA BA'I\
DBANG PO DPON SLOB GU nA MA TI DANG, RANG GI GRVA RGAN BLA MA\
SNGAGS RAMS PA DPAL 'BAR GNYIS KYIS LAM RIM MCHOD RTEN MAndAL\
CHE LEGS 'BUL TSAN DANG\

@068A *, ,BCAS TE BSKUL BA'I NGOR BKRA SHIS SGO MANG NAS DBU\
BTZUGS, SKABS LNGA BA YAN GRUB CING, RGYAL BAS LUNG BSTAN PA'I\
CHOS GRVA CHEN BO BKRA SHIS 'KHYIL DU RDZOGS BA'I? SANGS RGYAS\
ZIL GNON ME\
\
RTAR SKU BLTAMS NAS LO NYIS STONG DRUG BRGYA DANG SO GSUM, SANGS\
RGYAS SHING CHOS 'KHOR BSKOR NAS NYIS STONG LNGA BRGYA DANG GO\
BRGYAD LON PA RNAM 'BYANG ZHES PAS PHO KHYI'I LO MGO ZLA BA'I\
LNGA MCHOD CHEN MO'I DUS SU,\
\
SH'AKYA'I DGE SLONG MANG THOS 'JAM DBYANGS BZHAD PA'I RDO RJES\
SBYAR BA 'DIS KYANG RGYAL BA'I BSTAN PA PHYOGS DUS KUN TU DAR\

'DZIN THOS BSAM BRGYUD, NYI HONG MI RIGS SBYIN BDAG HA?\

KHO SING, HA YA MA SING NANG MI DANG BCAS PA, THA KHE MO RA\
SING, PA CIN ZHIG TZE NANG MI DANG BCAS PA, LI NA RI MIN, LE'O\
SING, SENG GA PUR MI RIGS HONG? PHRO YIN BCAS KYI MTHUN RKYEN\
